### [1] [GoCoMA: Hyperbolic Multimodal Representation Fusion for Large Language Model-Generated Code Attribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16377)
*Nitin Choudhury,Bikrant Bikram Pratap Maurya,Bhavinkumar Vinodbhai Kuwar,Arun Balaji Buduru*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: GoCoMA是一个多模态框架，通过结合代码风格特征和二进制预执行工件的图像表示，在双曲空间中融合多模态信息，用于LLM代码来源归属检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着LLM生成的代码越来越难以与人类编写的代码区分，这带来了安全漏洞和许可模糊等实际问题，因此需要解决"谁（或哪个LLM）写了这段代码？"的取证问题。

Method: GoCoMA采用多模态框架，建模代码风格特征（高层次结构风格签名）和二进制预执行工件图像表示（低层次执行导向字节语义）之间的外在层次关系。将模态嵌入投影到双曲庞加莱球中，通过基于测地线余弦相似度的跨模态注意力机制融合，然后将融合表示反投影到欧几里得空间进行最终LLM来源归属。

Result: 在两个开源基准测试（CoDET-M4和LLMAuthorBench）上的实验表明，GoCoMA在相同的评估协议下始终优于单模态和欧几里得多模态基线方法。

Conclusion: GoCoMA通过结合代码风格特征和二进制预执行工件的多模态表示，在双曲空间中有效融合不同层次的信息，为LLM代码来源归属提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) trained on massive code corpora are now increasingly capable of generating code that is hard to distinguish from human-written code. This raises practical concerns, including security vulnerabilities and licensing ambiguity, and also motivates a forensic question: 'Who (or which LLM) wrote this piece of code?' We present GoCoMA, a multimodal framework that models an extrinsic hierarchy between (i) code stylometry, capturing higher-level structural and stylistic signatures, and (ii) image representations of binary pre-executable artifacts (BPEA), capturing lower-level, execution-oriented byte semantics shaped by compilation and toolchains. GoCoMA projects modality embeddings into a hyperbolic Poincaré ball, fuses them via a geodesic-cosine similarity-based cross-modal attention (GCSA) fusion mechanism, and back-projects the fused representation to Euclidean space for final LLM-source attribution. Experiments on two open-source benchmarks (CoDET-M4 and LLMAuthorBench) show that GoCoMA consistently outperforms unimodal and Euclidean multimodal baselines under identical evaluation protocols.

</details>


### [2] [Reciprocal Co-Training (RCT): Coupling Gradient-Based and Non-Differentiable Models via Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16378)
*Yunshuo Tian,Akayou Kitessa,Tanuja Chitnis,Yijun Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出一个互惠协同训练框架，通过强化学习将LLM与随机森林分类器耦合，创建迭代反馈循环，使两种不同范式模型相互提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLMs）和传统机器学习方法（如随机森林）在预测建模中各有优势，但它们的表示形式和训练范式根本不同，阻碍了有效集成：LLMs基于文本数据的梯度优化，而随机森林使用不可微的特征划分。

Method: 提出互惠协同训练框架，通过强化学习将LLM与随机森林分类器耦合。将表格数据转换为标准化文本表示供LLM使用，LLM的嵌入增强随机森林特征空间，同时校准的随机森林概率估计为LLM的强化学习更新提供反馈信号。

Result: 在三个医学数据集上的实验表明，两种模型都获得了持续的性能提升，特别是LLM效果显著。消融分析显示迭代细化、混合奖励设计和维度控制共同促成了这些增益。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一种通用机制，允许不兼容的模型家族通过双向适应相互利用对方的优势。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) and classical machine learning methods offer complementary strengths for predictive modeling, yet their fundamentally different representations and training paradigms hinder effective integration: LLMs rely on gradient-based optimization over textual data, whereas models such as Random Forests (RF) employ non-differentiable feature partitioning. This work introduces a reciprocal co-training framework that couples an LLM with an RF classifier via reinforcement learning, creating an iterative feedback loop in which each model improves using signals from the other. Tabular data are reformulated into standardized textual representations for the LLM, whose embeddings augment the RF feature space, while calibrated RF probability estimates provide feedback signals that guide reinforcement learning updates of the LLM. Experiments across three medical datasets demonstrate consistent performance gains for both models, with particularly strong effects for the LLM. Ablation analyses show that iterative refinement, hybrid reward design, and dimensionality control jointly contribute to these gains. The proposed framework provides a general mechanism that allows incompatible model families to leverage each other's strengths through bidirectional adaptation.

</details>


### [3] [AdaExplore: Failure-Driven Adaptation and Diversity-Preserving Search for Efficient Kernel Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16625)
*Weihua Du,Jingming Zhuo,Yixin Dong,Andre Wang He,Weiwei Sun,Zeyu Zheng,Manupa Karunaratne,Ivan Fox,Tim Dettmers,Tianqi Chen,Yiming Yang,Sean Welleck*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: AdaExplore是一个LLM代理框架，通过积累执行反馈实现自我改进，专门用于高性能内核代码生成，包含失败驱动适应和多样性保持搜索两个阶段，在Triton等特定领域语言中显著提升正确性和优化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM代理在处理特定领域语言（如Triton）时面临挑战：这些语言在预训练数据中代表性不足，具有严格约束和非线性优化空间，导致朴素生成和局部细化不可靠。当前方法大多独立处理每个问题实例，无法积累可重用知识，限制了自我改进能力。

Method: AdaExplore采用两阶段框架：1) 失败驱动适应阶段：代理合成任务，将重复失败转换为可重用的有效性规则记忆，确保后续生成保持在可行集内；2) 多样性保持搜索阶段：将候选内核组织为树结构，交替进行局部细化和结构再生，探索超越局部最优的优化空间。

Result: 在KernelBench基准测试中，AdaExplore在100步内实现Level-2 3.12倍和Level-3 1.72倍的加速比，且随着计算资源增加持续改进，无需额外微调或外部知识。

Conclusion: AdaExplore通过积累执行反馈实现自我改进，有效解决了特定领域语言代码生成的挑战，在正确性和优化性能方面均取得显著提升，为LLM代理在性能关键代码生成领域的应用提供了新思路。

Abstract: Recent large language model (LLM) agents have shown promise in using execution feedback for test-time adaptation. However, robust self-improvement remains far from solved: most approaches still treat each problem instance independently, without accumulating reusable knowledge. This limitation is particularly pronounced in domain-specific languages such as Triton, which are underrepresented in LLM pretraining data. Their strict constraints and non-linear optimization landscape further make naive generation and local refinement unreliable. We propose AdaExplore, an agent framework that enables self-improvement via accumulated execution feedback for performance-critical kernel code generation through two complementary stages: failure-driven adaptation and diversity-preserving search, jointly improving correctness and optimization performance without additional fine-tuning or external knowledge. In the adaptation stage, the agent synthesizes tasks and converts recurring failures into a reusable memory of validity rules, helping subsequent generations remain within the feasible set. In the search stage, the agent organizes candidate kernels as a tree and alternates between small local refinements and larger structural regeneration, allowing it to explore the optimization landscape beyond local optima. Experiments on kernel runtime optimization benchmarks validate these gains: AdaExplore achieves 3.12x and 1.72x speedups on KernelBench Level-2 and Level-3, respectively, within 100 steps, and continues to improve with additional computation.

</details>


### [4] [Expressing Social Emotions: Misalignment Between LLMs and Human Cultural Emotion Norms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16757)
*Sree Bhattacharyya,Manas Mehta,Leona Chen,Cristina Salvador,Agata Lapedriza,Shiran Dudy,James Z. Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 研究发现当前LLM在表达社会情感时存在系统性文化错位，特别是过度表达"参与型"情感而忽视"脱离型"情感，且响应缺乏人类反应的多样性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着LLM越来越多地用于模拟跨文化互动中的人类行为，需要评估它们是否能准确捕捉人类表达社会情感的文化差异模式，因为文化错位的响应会降低其实用性。

Method: 提出心理学启发的跨文化社会情感表达评估框架，通过人类研究比较欧美和拉丁美洲参与者的情感表达，评估六个前沿LLM反映文化差异模式的能力。

Result: 发现模型与人类行为存在系统性错位：所有模型都更倾向于表达参与型而非脱离型情感，尤其在欧洲美国人设中差异显著；LLM响应高度集中且确定性，缺乏人类响应的多样性。

Conclusion: 当前LLM在表示文化与情感轴交互方面存在局限，特别是在表达社会情感时，这对它们在跨文化情感场景中的部署有直接影响。

Abstract: The expression of emotions that serve social purposes, such as asserting independence or fostering interdependence, is central to human interactions and varies systematically across cultures. As LLMs are increasingly used to simulate human behavior in culturally nuanced interactions, it is important to understand whether they faithfully capture human patterns of social emotion expression. When LLM responses are not culturally aligned, their utility is compromised -- particularly when users assume they are interacting with a culturally attuned interlocutor, and may act on advice that proves inappropriate in their cultural context. We present a psychologically informed evaluation framework of cross-cultural social emotion expression in LLMs. Using a human study comparing European American and Latin American participants' expression of engaging and disengaging emotions, we evaluate six frontier LLMs on their ability to reflect culturally differentiated patterns for expressing social emotions. We find systematic misalignment between model and human behavior: all models express engaging emotions more than disengaging ones, with particularly stark differences observed for the generally well-represented European American persona. We further highlight that LLM responses are highly concentrated and deterministic, failing to capture the diversity of human responses in expressing social emotions. Our ablation analyses reveal that these patterns are robust to sampling temperatures, partially sensitive to prompt language, and dependent on the response elicitation format. Together, our findings highlight limitations in how current LLMs represent the interaction of cultural and emotional axes, particularly when expressing social emotions, with direct implications for their deployment in cross-cultural affective contexts.

</details>


### [5] [StageMem: Lifecycle-Managed Memory for Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16774)
*Jiarui Han*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: StageMem是一个生命周期管理的内存框架，将内存视为有状态过程而非被动存储库，通过三阶段内存（瞬时、工作、持久）和置信度/强度建模来解决LLM系统中内存控制的实际问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM系统的内存设计主要将其视为静态存储，无法有效处理实际部署中的内存控制问题，包括：保留过多不确定项、重要内容以错误顺序遗忘、用户对持久性缺乏信任等。

Method: 提出StageMem框架，将内存组织为三个阶段（瞬时、工作、持久），为每个内存项建模置信度和强度，实现从浅层准入到长期承诺的分离，支持信息在不同阶段间的提升、保留、更新或淘汰。

Result: 在受控压力机制下，该分解有助于保留后期重要内容，同时更好地控制内存负担和深层污染。适应外部任务提供边界证据表明相同模式与更强的检索结构兼容。

Conclusion: StageMem为语言模型系统提供了内存控制问题的原则性分解框架，将内存视为有状态过程而非被动存储库，解决了实际部署中的关键挑战。

Abstract: Long-horizon language model systems increasingly rely on persistent memory, yet many current designs still treat memory primarily as a static store: write an item, place it into memory, and retrieve it later if needed. We argue that this framing does not adequately capture the practical memory-control problem in deployed LLM systems. In realistic settings, the difficulty is often not merely forgetting useful information, but retaining too many uncertain items, forgetting important content in the wrong order, and giving users little trust in what will persist over time. We propose StageMem, a lifecycle-managed memory framework that treats memory as a stateful process rather than a passive repository. StageMem organizes memory into three stages -- transient, working, and durable memory -- and models each item with explicit confidence and strength. This separates shallow admission from long-term commitment: information may first be written at low cost and only later be promoted, retained, updated, or evicted as evidence and pressure evolve. Under controlled pressure regimes, this decomposition helps preserve late-important content while keeping memory burden and deeper-tier pollution more controlled. Adapted external tasks provide boundary evidence that the same schema remains compatible with stronger retrieval structure outside pure synthetic control. We present StageMem as a principled decomposition of the memory-control problem for language model systems.

</details>


### [6] [HeLa-Mem: Hebbian Learning and Associative Memory for LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16839)
*Jinchang Zhu,Jindong Li,Cheng Zhang,Jiahong Liu,Menglin Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出HeLa-Mem，一种受生物启发的记忆架构，通过动态图和赫布学习模拟人类记忆的关联、巩固和扩散激活机制，解决LLM智能体长期记忆问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体的记忆系统将对话历史表示为非结构化嵌入向量，通过语义相似性检索信息，无法捕捉人类记忆的关联结构。生物记忆中的关联、巩固和扩散激活机制在当前研究中基本缺失。

Method: 提出HeLa-Mem架构：1) 情景记忆图通过共激活模式演化；2) 语义记忆存储通过赫布蒸馏填充，其中反思智能体识别密集连接的记忆枢纽并将其提炼为结构化、可重用的语义知识。采用双路径设计，结合语义相似性和学习到的关联。

Result: 在LoCoMo基准测试中，在四个问题类别上表现出优越性能，同时使用显著更少的上下文token。

Conclusion: HeLa-Mem通过模拟生物记忆机制，有效解决了LLM智能体的长期记忆挑战，在保持对话连贯性和知识重用方面优于现有方法。

Abstract: Long-term memory is a critical challenge for Large Language Model agents, as fixed context windows cannot preserve coherence across extended interactions. Existing memory systems represent conversation history as unstructured embedding vectors, retrieving information through semantic similarity. This paradigm fails to capture the associative structure of human memory, wherein related experiences progressively strengthen interconnections through repeated co-activation. Inspired by cognitive neuroscience, we identify three mechanisms central to biological memory: association, consolidation, and spreading activation, which remain largely absent in current research.
  To bridge this gap, we propose HeLa-Mem, a bio-inspired memory architecture that models memory as a dynamic graph with Hebbian learning dynamics. HeLa-Mem employs a dual-level organization: (1) an episodic memory graph that evolves through co-activation patterns, and (2) a semantic memory store populated via Hebbian Distillation, wherein a Reflective Agent identifies densely connected memory hubs and distills them into structured, reusable semantic knowledge. This dual-path design leverages both semantic similarity and learned associations, mirroring the episodic-semantic distinction in human cognition. Experiments on LoCoMo demonstrate superior performance across four question categories while using significantly fewer context tokens. Code is available on GitHub: https://github.com/ReinerBRO/HeLa-Mem

</details>


### [7] [Freshness-Aware Prioritized Experience Replay for LLM/VLM Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16918)
*Weiyu Ma,Yongcheng Zeng,Yan Song,Xinyu Cui,Jian Zhao,Xuhui Liu,Mohamed Elhoseiny*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出Freshness-Aware PER方法，通过引入指数年龄衰减解决LLM/VLM强化学习中优先经验回放的优先级过时问题，显著提升样本效率


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM/VLM强化学习主要使用PPO、GRPO等on-policy算法，这些方法在单次梯度更新后丢弃所有收集的轨迹，导致样本效率低下。虽然经典RL中经验回放能提高样本效率，但直接应用于LLM会因策略快速演变导致存储的优先级过时，使旧的高优先级轨迹长期主导采样

Method: 提出Freshness-Aware PER方法，基于有效样本量分析，在任意PER优先级基础上添加乘性指数年龄衰减，解决优先级过时问题。这是首个成功将PER应用于LLM/VLM强化学习的工作

Result: 在8个多步agentic、推理和数学竞赛任务上评估0.5B、3B和7B模型。Freshness-Aware PER显著优于on-policy基线：NQ Search提升46%，Sokoban提升367%，VLM FrozenLake提升133%。而标准PER（无年龄衰减）始终降低性能

Conclusion: Freshness-Aware PER成功解决了LLM/VLM强化学习中PER的优先级过时问题，显著提高了样本效率，在多个任务上取得了显著性能提升

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning (RL) has achieved impressive success in post-training Large Language Models (LLMs) and Vision-Language Models (VLMs), with on-policy algorithms such as PPO, GRPO, and REINFORCE++ serving as the dominant paradigm. However, these methods discard all collected trajectories after a single gradient update, resulting in poor sample efficiency, particularly wasteful for agentic tasks where multi-turn environment interactions are expensive. While Experience Replay drives sample efficiency in classic RL by allowing agents to reuse past trajectories and prioritize informative ones, directly applying Prioritized Experience Replay (PER) to LLMs fails. The rapid policy evolution of billion-parameter models renders stored priorities stale, causing old high-priority trajectories to dominate sampling long after they have become uninformative. We propose Freshness-Aware PER, which addresses this priority staleness problem by augmenting any PER-based priority with a multiplicative exponential age decay grounded in effective sample size analysis. To the best of our knowledge, Freshness-Aware PER is the first work to successfully apply PER to LLM/VLM reinforcement learning. We evaluate on eight multi-step agentic, reasoning, and math competition tasks with 0.5B, 3B, and 7B models. Freshness-Aware PER significantly outperforms on-policy baselines, achieving +46% on NQ Search, +367% on Sokoban, and +133% on VLM FrozenLake, while standard PER without age decay consistently degrades performance. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/Vision-CAIR/Freshness-Aware-PER.

</details>


### [8] [Bolzano: Case Studies in LLM-Assisted Mathematical Research](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16989)
*Jan Grebík,Pavel Hubáček,Martin Koutecký,Matěj Kripner,Václav Rozhoň,Robert Šámal,Adrián Zámečník*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Bolzano多智能体LLM系统在数学和理论计算机科学中取得了6个新成果，其中4个达到可发表研究水平，3个基本由系统自主完成


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索大型语言模型在数学研究中的实际应用潜力，验证多智能体系统能否产生有意义的数学研究成果

Method: 使用Bolzano开源多智能体LLM系统，通过证明者智能体和验证者智能体之间的并行交互轮次，维护跨轮次的持久知识库

Result: 在数学和理论计算机科学中产生了6个新结果，其中4个达到可发表研究水平，3个基本由系统自主完成

Conclusion: LLM能够在数学研究中做出有意义的贡献，补充了近期其他研究团队的发现

Abstract: We report new results on six problems in mathematics and theoretical computer science, produced with the assistance of Bolzano, an open-source multi-agent LLM system. Bolzano orchestrates rounds of interaction between parallel prover agents and a verifier agent while maintaining a persistent knowledge base that is carried across rounds. Classified using the significance-autonomy taxonomy of Feng et al., four of the six results reach the level of publishable research, and three of the six were produced essentially autonomously by Bolzano. Our results provide evidence that LLMs can contribute meaningfully to mathematical research, complementing recent reports by Bubeck et al., Woodruff et al., and others.

</details>


### [9] [SPS: Steering Probability Squeezing for Better Exploration in Reinforcement Learning for Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16995)
*Yifu Huo,Chenglong Wang,Ziming Zhu,Shunjie Xing,Peinan Feng,Tongran Liu,Qiaozhi He,Tianhua Zhou,Xiaojia Chang,Jingbo Zhu,Zhengtao Yu,Tong Xiao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出SPS训练范式，通过交替使用强化学习和逆强化学习来解决RL训练中概率质量过度集中在少数高奖励轨迹的问题，从而增强探索能力并提升多样本推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统强化学习训练推理模型时，虽然能提高单样本成功率（Pass@1），但探索能力有限，导致多样化的推理轨迹不足，限制了多样本性能（Pass@k）。研究发现这是由于概率质量过度集中在少数高奖励轨迹上的"挤压效应"所致。

Method: 提出Steering Probability Squeezing (SPS)训练范式，交替使用常规强化学习和逆强化学习。将策略rollout视为演示数据，利用IRL显式地重塑轨迹分布，从而增强探索能力，无需外部监督。

Result: 在五个常用推理基准测试上的实验表明，SPS能够实现更好的探索并提升Pass@k性能。研究还分析了RL学习动态，识别了Pass@k的实证上限，揭示了RL推理模型的内在探索限制。

Conclusion: 在强化学习和逆强化学习之间交替提供了一条有效途径，可以扩展推理导向大语言模型的探索能力。SPS通过重塑轨迹分布解决了概率挤压问题，为提升多样本推理性能提供了新方法。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as a promising paradigm for training reasoning-oriented models by leveraging rule-based reward signals. However, RL training typically tends to improve single-sample success rates (i.e., Pass@1) while offering limited exploration of diverse reasoning trajectories, which is crucial for multi-sample performance (i.e., Pass@k). Our preliminary analysis reveals that this limitation stems from a fundamental squeezing effect, whereby probability mass is excessively concentrated on a narrow subset of high-reward trajectories, restricting genuine exploration and constraining attainable performance under RL training. To address this issue, in this work, we propose Steering Probability Squeezing (SPS), a training paradigm that interleaves conventional RL with inverse reinforcement learning (IRL). SPS treats on-policy rollouts as demonstrations and employs IRL to explicitly reshape the induced trajectory distribution, thereby enhancing exploration without introducing external supervision. Experiments on five commonly used reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that SPS can enable better exploration and improve Pass@k. Beyond algorithmic contributions, we provide an analysis of RL learning dynamics and identify an empirical upper bound on Pass@k, shedding light on intrinsic exploration limits in RL-based reasoning models. Our findings suggest that alternating between RL and IRL offers an effective pathway toward extending the exploration capacity of reasoning-oriented large language models.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对支持性LLM的评估大多基于单轮、完全指定的提示，而用户实际寻求社会支持时是逐步披露情况的，这种评估方式存在差距。

Method: 引入多轮模拟框架：从五个Reddit社区收集支持寻求叙事，分解为有序片段逐轮呈现给语言模型；使用社会支持行为编码(SSBC)对响应进行多标签分类；通过线性探针在隐藏表示上估计模型内部对用户痛苦的感知。

Result: 支持策略随估计的痛苦程度系统性变化：随着估计痛苦上升，教学策略下降（这一发现在不同架构中可复现）；情感和自尊导向策略（如验证）增加但模型特异性强且标注噪声大；社区背景独立影响行为，反映话题和话语规范而非人口统计类别。

Conclusion: 单轮评估无法捕捉的轨迹级动态表明，需要为社交敏感应用开发多轮审计框架。

Abstract: When users seek social support from chatbots, they disclose their situation gradually, yet most evaluations of supportive LLMs rely on single-turn, fully specified prompts. We introduce a multi-turn simulation framework that closes this gap. Support-seeking narratives from five Reddit communities are decomposed into ordered fragments and revealed turn by turn to a language model. Each response is coded with the Social Support Behavior Code (SSBC), an established multi-label taxonomy that captures the composition of support, rather than a single quality score. To ask whether support choices track the model's own construal of user distress, we use linear probes on hidden representations to estimate this internal signal without altering the generation context. Across two mid-scale models (Llama-3.1-8B, OLMo-3-7B) and more than 6,200 turns, support composition shifts systematically with estimated distress: teaching declines as estimated distress rises, a finding that replicates across architectures, while increases in affective and esteem-oriented strategies (such as validation) are suggestive but model-specific and rest on noisier annotations. Community context independently shapes behavior, tracking topic and discourse norms rather than demographic categories. These trajectory-level dynamics, invisible to single-turn evaluation, motivate multi-turn auditing frameworks for socially sensitive applications.

### [12] [GenericAgent: A Token-Efficient Self-Evolving LLM Agent via Contextual Information Density Maximization (V1.0)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17091)
*Jiaqing Liang,Jinyi Han,Weijia Li,Xinyi Wang,Zhoujia Zhang,Zishang Jiang,Ying Liao,Tingyun Li,Ying Huang,Hao Shen,Hanyu Wu,Fang Guo,Keyi Wang,Zhonghua Hong,Zhiyu Lu,Lipeng Ma,Sihang Jiang,Yanghua Xiao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: GenericAgent (GA) 是一个基于上下文信息密度最大化原则的通用自进化LLM智能体系统，通过最小化工具集、分层按需记忆、自我进化机制和上下文压缩等技术，在有限上下文预算内提升决策相关信息密度，显著优于现有系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前长时程LLM智能体受限于上下文长度，随着交互变长，工具描述、记忆检索和环境反馈会挤占决策所需信息，同时有用经验在任务间丢失。作者认为长时程性能不应由上下文长度决定，而应由有限上下文预算内保持的决策相关信息密度决定。

Method: GA围绕上下文信息密度最大化原则构建四个核心组件：1) 最小原子工具集保持接口简单；2) 分层按需记忆默认只显示高层视图；3) 自我进化机制将已验证轨迹转化为可重用SOP和可执行代码；4) 上下文截断和压缩层在执行过程中保持信息密度。

Result: 在任务完成、工具使用效率、记忆有效性、自我进化和网页浏览等方面，GA始终优于领先的智能体系统，同时使用显著更少的token和交互次数，并且能够随时间持续进化。

Conclusion: 长时程LLM智能体的性能瓶颈在于上下文信息密度而非长度，GA通过系统化设计实现了信息密度最大化，为构建高效、可扩展的智能体系统提供了新范式。

Abstract: Long-horizon large language model (LLM) agents are fundamentally limited by context. As interactions become longer, tool descriptions, retrieved memories, and raw environmental feedback accumulate and push out the information needed for decision-making. At the same time, useful experience gained from tasks is often lost across episodes. We argue that long-horizon performance is determined not by context length, but by how much decision-relevant information is maintained within a finite context budget. We present GenericAgent (GA), a general-purpose, self-evolving LLM agent system built around a single principle: context information density maximization. GA implements this through four closely connected components: a minimal atomic tool set that keeps the interface simple, a hierarchical on-demand memory that only shows a small high-level view by default, a self-evolution mechanism that turns verified past trajectories into reusable SOPs and executable code, and a context truncation and compression layer that maintains information density during long executions. Across task completion, tool use efficiency, memory effectiveness, self-evolution, and web browsing, GA consistently outperforms leading agent systems while using significantly fewer tokens and interactions, and it continues to evolve over time. Project: https://github.com/lsdefine/GenericAgent

### [13] [The Consensus Trap: Rescuing Multi-Agent LLMs from Adversarial Majorities via Token-Level Collaboration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17139)
*Jiayuan Liu,Shiyi Du,Weihua Du,Mingyu Guo,Vincent Conitzer*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文揭示当前多智能体LLM系统中基于多数投票的响应级聚合存在结构性漏洞：当被恶意污染的智能体形成局部多数时，系统会崩溃。作者提出令牌级轮询协作方法，通过智能体在共享自回归上下文中顺序交错生成令牌，将聚合从脆弱的最终投票计数转变为动态交织的逻辑链，从而在恶意智能体占多数时仍能保持鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多智能体LLM架构依赖响应级聚合（如多数投票）来提升推理能力，但在开放环境中，智能体容易受到隐蔽的上下文污染（如针对性提示注入）。研究发现当被污染的智能体形成局部多数时，这种聚合机制会崩溃，因为投票只关注最终结论而忽略有缺陷的中间逻辑。

Method: 提出令牌级轮询协作方法：智能体在共享自回归上下文中顺序交错生成令牌，将这一过程形式化为离散时间动态系统。理论分析表明，令牌级交错将聚合从线性求和（最终投票计数）转变为非线性算子乘积（动态交织的逻辑链），使诚实模型的恢复力能够克服对抗性污染。

Result: 在多个推理基准测试中进行全面实证评估，结果显示：当被污染的智能体达到多数时，多数投票方法崩溃，而轮询协作方法在超过这一关键阈值后仍能保持鲁棒的准确性。

Conclusion: 令牌级轮询协作通过将聚合从响应级转移到令牌级，解决了多智能体LLM系统的结构性漏洞，即使在恶意智能体占多数的情况下也能保持系统鲁棒性，为构建更安全的协作AI系统提供了新方向。

Abstract: Multi-agent large language model (LLM) architectures increasingly rely on response-level aggregation, such as Majority Voting (MAJ), to raise reasoning ceilings. However, in open environments, agents are highly susceptible to stealthy contextual corruption, such as targeted prompt injections. We reveal a critical structural vulnerability in current multi-agent systems: response-level aggregation collapses when corrupted agents form a local majority. Because voting aggregates fully-formed conclusions, it is blind to flawed intermediate logic. To overcome this systematic limitation, we propose the Token-Level Round-Robin (RR) Collaboration, where agents sequentially interleave generation within a shared auto-regressive context. We formalize this process as a discrete-time dynamical system, proving that token-level interleaving transitions aggregation from a brittle counting of final votes (a linear sum) to a dynamic, interwoven chain of logic (a non-linear operator product). Through this theoretical lens, we prove that the honest model's restorative pull can overpower adversarial corruptions, even when corrupted agents form a majority. We conduct an exhaustive empirical evaluation across diverse reasoning benchmarks and demonstrate that while MAJ collapses when corrupted agents reach a majority, RR maintains robust accuracy well beyond this critical threshold.

</details>


### [14] [Modeling Multi-Dimensional Cognitive States in Large Language Models under Cognitive Crowding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17174)
*Lin Zhong,Siyu Zhu,Zizhen Yuan,Jinhao Cui,Xinyang Zhao,Lingzhi Wang,Hao Chen,Qing Liao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了CognitiveBench基准测试和HyCoLLM方法，用于解决LLMs在多维度认知状态联合建模中的性能瓶颈问题


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLMs主要处理孤立任务（如情感分析或立场检测），无法捕捉心理学中定义的多个认知维度（情感、思维方式、立场、意图）之间的交互作用

Method: 1) 构建CognitiveBench基准测试，统一标注四个认知维度；2) 使用Gromov δ-双曲性分析发现基准的层次结构；3) 提出HyCoLLM方法，在双曲空间中建模认知状态，通过双曲引导对齐调优对齐LLM表示

Result: LLMs在单维度任务上表现良好，但在联合多维度建模中性能急剧下降；HyCoLLM显著改善了多维度认知理解，使8B参数模型能够超越包括GPT-4o在内的强大基线

Conclusion: 认知状态具有层次结构，在欧几里得空间中需要指数级表示空间，导致"认知拥挤"问题；在双曲空间中建模认知状态可以有效解决这一表示瓶颈

Abstract: Modeling human cognitive states is essential for advanced artificial intelligence. Existing Large Language Models (LLMs) mainly address isolated tasks such as emotion analysis or stance detection, and fail to capture interactions among cognitive dimensions defined in psychology, including emotion, thinking style, stance, and intention. To bridge this gap, we construct CognitiveBench, the first benchmark with unified annotations across the above four dimensions. Experiments on CognitiveBench show that although LLMs perform well on single dimension tasks, their performance drops sharply in joint multi-dimensional modeling. Using Gromov $δ$-hyperbolicity analysis, we find that CognitiveBench exhibits a strong hierarchical structure. We attribute the performance bottleneck to ``Cognitive Crowding'', where hierarchical cognitive states require exponential representational space, while the Euclidean space of LLMs grows only polynomially, causing representation overlap and degraded performance. To address this mismatch, we propose HyCoLLM, which models cognitive states in hyperbolic space and aligns LLM representations via Hyperbolic Guided Alignment Tuning. Results show that HyCoLLM substantially improves multi-dimensional cognitive understanding, allowing 8B parameter model to outperform strong baselines, including GPT-4o.

Method: 提出MACE多智能体框架，包含三个专门智能体：规划器（生成推理策略）、执行器（提供详细计算步骤）、验证器（验证逻辑）。每个智能体采用零样本思维链设置执行任务，无需复杂微调，产生可解释的验证追踪。

Abstract: We present a novel approach for claim verification from tabular data documents. Recent LLM-based approaches either employ complex pretraining/fine-tuning or decompose verification into subtasks, often lacking comprehensive explanations and generalizability. To address these limitations, we propose a Multi-Agentic framework for Claim verification (MACE) consisting of three specialized agents: Planner, Executor, and Verifier. Instead of elaborate finetuning, each agent employs a zero-shot Chain-of-Thought setup to perform its tasks. MACE produces interpretable verification traces, with the Planner generating explicit reasoning strategies, the Executor providing detailed computation steps, and the Verifier validating the logic. Experiments demonstrate that MACE achieves state-of-the-art (SOTA) performance on two datasets and performs on par with the best models on two others, while achieving 80--100\% of best performance with substantially smaller models: 27--92B parameters versus 235B. This combination of competitive performance, memory efficiency, and transparent reasoning highlights our framework's effectiveness.

### [16] [DORA Explorer: Improving the Exploration Ability of LLMs Without Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17244)
*Priya Gurjar,Md Farhan Ishmam,Kenneth Marino*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: DORA Explorer是一个无需训练、提升LLM智能体探索多样性的框架，通过生成多样化候选动作、基于token对数概率评分、可调探索参数选择动作，在MAB和TALES环境中表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM智能体在序列决策中输出多样性不足，导致探索不充分、收敛到次优解、陷入循环，特别是在需要主动探索收集信息的环境中。现有方法如温度缩放只能引入token级随机性，无法在序列层面产生足够多样性。

Method: 提出DORA Explorer框架：1) 生成多样化动作候选；2) 使用token对数概率为候选动作评分；3) 通过可调探索参数选择动作。该框架无需额外训练，可提升LLM智能体的探索能力。

Result: 在经典多臂老虎机(MAB)和文本冒险学习环境套件(TALES)中评估：DORA在MAB上达到UCB竞争性性能，在TALES中取得一致增益，例如将Qwen2.5-7B在TextWorld中的性能从29.2%提升到45.5%。

Conclusion: DORA Explorer有效解决了LLM智能体探索多样性不足的问题，无需训练即可显著提升探索性能，在多种决策环境中表现出色。

Abstract: Despite the rapid progress, LLMs for sequential decision-making (i.e., LLM agents) still struggle to produce diverse outputs. This leads to insufficient exploration, convergence to sub-optimal solutions, and becoming stuck in loops. Such limitations can be problematic in environments that require active exploration to gather information and make decisions. Sampling methods such as temperature scaling introduce token-level randomness but fail to produce enough diversity at the sequence level. We analyze LLM exploration in the classic Multi-Armed Bandit (MAB) setting and the Text Adventure Learning Environment Suite (TALES). We find that current decoding strategies and prompting methods like Chain-of-Thought and Tree-of-Thought are insufficient for robust exploration. To address this, we introduce DORA Explorer (Diversity-Oriented Ranking of Actions), a training-free framework for improving exploration in LLM agents. DORA generates diverse action candidates, scores them using token log-probabilities, and selects actions using a tunable exploration parameter. DORA achieves UCB-competitive performance on MAB and consistent gains across TALES, e.g., improving Qwen2.5-7B's performance from 29.2% to 45.5% in TextWorld. Our project is available at: https://dora-explore.github.io/.

### [17] [Seeing Isn't Believing: Mitigating Belief Inertia via Active Intervention in Embodied Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17252)
*Hanlin Wang,Chak Tou Leong,Jian Wang,Wenjie Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出EVU机制解决智能体信念惯性问题，通过预测-验证-更新流程主动管理信念，在具身任务中显著提升成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于大语言模型的智能体在复杂具身任务中常做出次优决策，原因是它们忽视与环境反馈不符的关键信息，表现为"信念惯性"——智能体固执坚持先验信念而忽略明确观察。

Method: 提出Estimate-Verify-Update (EVU)机制：1) 预测预期结果；2) 通过显式推理验证观察与预测的一致性；3) 基于验证证据主动更新先验信念。EVU生成文本化信念状态，可集成到基于提示和基于训练的智能体推理方法中。

Result: 在三个具身基准测试上的广泛实验表明，EVU持续带来任务成功率的显著提升。进一步分析验证了该方法有效缓解信念惯性问题。

Conclusion: EVU机制通过主动信念干预解决智能体信念惯性问题，推动了更鲁棒具身智能体的发展。该方法可作为统一干预机制应用于不同推理方法。

Abstract: Recent advancements in large language models (LLMs) have enabled agents to tackle complex embodied tasks through environmental interaction. However, these agents still make suboptimal decisions and perform ineffective actions, as they often overlook critical environmental feedback that differs from their internal beliefs. Through a formal probing analysis, we characterize this as belief inertia, a phenomenon where agents stubbornly adhere to prior beliefs despite explicit observations. To address this, we advocate active belief intervention, moving from passive understanding to active management. We introduce the Estimate-Verify-Update (EVU) mechanism, which empowers agents to predict expected outcomes, verify them against observations through explicit reasoning, and actively update prior beliefs based on the verification evidence. EVU is designed as a unified intervention mechanism that generates textual belief states explicitly, and can be integrated into both prompting-based and training-based agent reasoning methods. Extensive experiments across three embodied benchmarks demonstrate that EVU consistently yields substantial gains in task success rates. Further analyses validate that our approach effectively mitigates belief inertia, advancing the development of more robust embodied agents. Our code is available at https://github.com/WangHanLinHenry/EVU.

</details>


### [18] [Probabilistic Programs of Thought](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17290)
*Poorva Garg,Renato Lui Geh,Daniel Israel,Todd Millstein,Kyle Richardson,Guy Van den Broeck*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出Probabilistic Programs of Thought框架，通过将LLM生成的程序转换为概率程序，在不增加GPU计算的情况下获得更多样本，提高代码生成和数学推理的效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前代码生成方法需要多次采样LLM，每次采样都需要GPU计算，当需要大量样本时计算成本过高。需要一种方法能在不增加GPU计算的情况下获得更多程序样本。

Method: 提出Probabilistic Programs of Thought框架：1) 从LLM生成一个程序并获取其下一个token的概率分布；2) 构建一个概率程序，紧凑地表示指数级的确定性程序；3) 在概率程序中进行概率推理，以极低的CPU开销采样新程序。

Result: 在代码生成、代码理解和数学推理基准测试中，该方法在减少LLM生成次数的情况下提高了性能表现。

Conclusion: 通过将LLM分布嵌入到生成程序中，构建概率程序的方法能够显著减少GPU计算需求，同时获得更多程序样本，为代码生成和数学推理任务提供了更高效的解决方案。

Abstract: LLMs are widely used for code generation and mathematical reasoning tasks where they are required to generate structured output. They either need to reason about code, generate code for a given specification, or reason using programs of thought. The typical approach to code generation is to prompt the model and generate samples until an appropriate program is obtained. Within this process, sampling $n$ programs from the language model requires $n$ GPU compute-intensive generations which becomes prohibitively expensive for larger values of $n$. In this work, we address this limitation by exposing the LLM's distribution within the generated programs themselves. We propose a novel test-time framework we dub probabilistic programs of thought to obtain more samples from the model with fewer LLM generations. Given a program generated by a model and the associated next-token probabilities, we build a probabilistic program that compactly represents exponentially many deterministic programs. Since performing probabilistic reasoning in this probabilistic program is much cheaper, our approach allows sampling new programs without any additional GPU compute and little CPU overhead. We instantiate our approach on benchmarks for code generation, code understanding and mathematical reasoning and report improvements in performance with fewer generations from the LLM.

</details>


### [19] [Beyond "I Don't Know": Evaluating LLM Self-Awareness in Discriminating Data and Model Uncertainty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17293)
*Jingyi Ren,Ante Wang,Yunghwei Lai,Xiaolong Wang,Linlu Gong,Weitao Li,Weizhi Ma,Yang Liu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究通常将LLMs的拒绝回答视为通用的"我不知道"，未能区分输入层面的模糊性（数据不确定性）和能力限制（模型不确定性）。这种缺乏区分限制了后续行动决策，如请求澄清或调用外部工具。

Abstract: Reliable Large Language Models (LLMs) should abstain when confidence is insufficient. However, prior studies often treat refusal as a generic "I don't know'', failing to distinguish input-level ambiguity (data uncertainty) from capability limitations (model uncertainty). This lack of distinction limits downstream action decisions like requesting clarification or invoking external tools. In this work, we introduce UA-Bench, a benchmark of over 3,500 questions drawn from six datasets spanning knowledge-intensive and reasoning-intensive tasks, designed to evaluate explicit uncertainty attribution. An evaluation of 18 frontier LLMs shows that even state-of-the-art models struggle to reliably discriminate between data uncertainty and model uncertainty, and that high answer accuracy does not necessarily imply strong uncertainty attribution ability. To narrow this gap, we propose a lightweight data synthesis and reinforcement learning strategy. Experiments on both Qwen3-4B-Instruct-2507 and Qwen3-8B in thinking mode show that the proposed method improves uncertainty attribution while preserving answer accuracy. ### [21] [AnchorMem: Anchored Facts with Associative Contexts for Building Memory in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17377)
*Zhanyu Shen,Sijie Cheng,Zhicheng Guo,Weiqin Wang,Yile Wang,Hui Huang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: AnchorMem是一种新颖的记忆框架，通过将检索单元与生成上下文解耦，使用原子事实作为检索锚点，同时保留原始上下文作为不可变背景，以解决现有记忆方法过度依赖总结而稀释关键上下文的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆方法（如A-Mem、Mem0）过度强调通过频繁重写来组织交互，这种对总结的严重依赖会稀释重要的上下文细微差别并模糊关键检索特征。需要一种能够平衡细粒度检索与上下文完整性的记忆系统。

Method: AnchorMem受认知科学中的普鲁斯特现象启发，提出将检索单元与生成上下文解耦的方法：1）从交互历史中提取原子事实作为检索锚点；2）保留原始上下文作为不可变背景；3）构建关联事件图，使用高阶事件链接将相关事实绑定到共享事件表示中；4）检索时，将查询锚定到特定事实和事件来定位相关记忆，但使用关联的原始块和事件重建上下文。

Result: 在LoCoMo基准测试上，对三个闭源和开源模型的实验表明，AnchorMem显著优于基线方法。

Conclusion: AnchorMem通过解耦检索单元与生成上下文，实现了细粒度检索与交互上下文完整性的调和，提供了一种更有效的长期交互记忆系统。

Abstract: While large language models have achieved remarkable performance in complex tasks, they still need a memory system to utilize historical experience in long-term interactions. Existing memory methods (e.g., A-Mem, Mem0) place excessive emphasis on organizing interactions by frequently rewriting them, however, this heavy reliance on summarization risks diluting essential contextual nuances and obscuring key retrieval features. To bridge this gap, we introduce AnchorMem, a novel memory framework inspired by the Proust Phenomenon in cognitive science, where a specific anchor triggers a holistic recollection. We propose a method that decouples the retrieval unit from the generation context. AnchorMem extracts atomic facts from interaction history to serve as retrieval anchors, while preserving the original context as the immutable context. To reveal implicit narrative cues, we construct an associative event graph that uses higher-order event links that bind sets of related facts into shared event representations, strengthening cross-memory integration without relying on generic entities as bridges. During retrieval, the system anchors queries to specific facts and events to locate relevant memories, but reconstructs the context using the associated raw chunks and events. Our method reconciles fine-grained retrieval with the contextual integrity of interactions. Experiments across three closed-source and open-source models on the LoCoMo benchmark demonstrate that AnchorMem significantly outperforms baselines. Code is available at https://github.com/RayNeo-AI-2025/AnchorMem.

</details>

*George Drayson*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Jupiter-N是基于开源模型Nemotron 3 Super构建的混合推理模型，通过不确定性轨迹、英国文化对齐和威尔士语支持进行后训练，在保持基础能力的同时在多个领域取得显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发一个能够同时具备智能体能力、特定文化对齐和语言支持的模型，为各国提供一个可复制的后训练模板，实现主权AI发展。

Method: 采用Forget-Me-Not框架，混合策略内合成回放和策略外任务数据防止灾难性遗忘；结合推理和非推理轨迹保持混合推理能力；使用不确定性轨迹提升智能体能力，基于文化规范的合成数据实现文化对齐，平行语料库和LLM翻译支持威尔士语。

Result: 在威尔士语任务上显著提升（ARC-Easy +18，MMLU-Lite +5.25），终端使用能力提升（Terminal Bench 2 +9.1），指令跟随能力提升（IFBench +4.4），同时保持了基础模型的核心能力。

Conclusion: Jupiter-N提供了一个可复制的后训练模板，通过替换文化知识、机构语料和目标语言，可以为任何国家构建类似的AI模型，所有模型权重和训练数据都已开源发布。

Abstract: We present Jupiter-N, a hybrid reasoning model post-trained from Nemotron 3 Super, a fully open-source 120 billion parameter LLM. We target three objectives: (1) agentic capability via uncertainty-curated trajectories; (2) UK cultural alignment via synthetic data grounded in cultural norms; and (3) Welsh language support via parallel corpora and LLM-translated Welsh conversations. Our data curation strategy carefully preserves the base model's capabilities: using our Forget-Me-Not framework, we mix on-policy synthetic replay with off-policy task data to mitigate catastrophic forgetting, and include a mixture of reasoning and non-reasoning traces to maintain Nemotron's hybrid reasoning ability. Jupiter-N achieves standout gains over Nemotron in Welsh (+18 on ARC-Easy, +5.25 on MMLU-Lite), terminal-use (+9.1 on Terminal Bench 2) and instruction following (+4.4 on IFBench), while retaining the base model capabilities. We frame this work as a reproducible template for sovereign post-training: substituting cultural knowledge, institutional corpora, and target languages produces an equivalent pipeline for any country. All model weights and all post-training datasets are publicly released under open licences.

### [23] [Answer Only as Precisely as Justified: Calibrated Claim-Level Specificity Control for Agentic Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17487)
*Tianyi Huang,Samuel Xu,Jason Tansong Dang,Samuel Yan,Kimberley Yin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出CSS方法，通过分解答案为具体主张、提出更粗略的回退版本，并在可接受范围内以最具体的校准级别输出每个主张，来解决智能体系统过度承诺的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 智能体系统经常失败不是因为完全错误，而是因为过于精确：回答可能整体有用，但某些具体主张超出了证据支持的范围。这种过度承诺问题是当前智能体系统的重要缺陷。

Method: 提出组合选择性特异性（CSS）方法，作为后生成层：1）将答案分解为具体主张；2）为每个主张提出更粗略的回退版本；3）在可接受范围内以最具体的校准级别输出每个主张。该方法将不确定性表达为局部语义回退而非整体拒绝。

Result: 在LongFact完整运行和HotpotQA试点中，校准的CSS改善了固定草稿的风险-效用权衡。在LongFact完整运行中，相对于无CSS输出，将过度承诺感知效用从0.846提升到0.913，同时达到0.938的特异性保留率。

Conclusion: 主张级特异性控制是智能体系统有用的不确定性接口，也是未来无分布有效性层的目标。该方法能有效平衡精确性和可靠性。

Abstract: Agentic systems often fail not by being entirely wrong, but by being too precise: a response may be generally useful while particular claims exceed what the evidence supports. We study this failure mode as overcommitment control and introduce compositional selective specificity (CSS), a post-generation layer that decomposes an answer into claims, proposes coarser backoffs, and emits each claim at the most specific calibrated level that appears admissible. The method is designed to express uncertainty as a local semantic backoff rather than as a whole-answer refusal. Across a full LongFact run and HotpotQA pilots, calibrated CSS improves the risk-utility trade-off of fixed drafts. On the full LongFact run, it raises overcommitment-aware utility from 0.846 to 0.913 relative to the no-CSS output while achieving 0.938 specificity retention. These results suggest that claim-level specificity control is a useful uncertainty interface for agentic systems and a target for future distribution-free validity layers.

</details>


### [24] [Agents Explore but Agents Ignore: LLMs Lack Environmental Curiosity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17609)
*Leon Engländer,Sophia Althammer,Ahmet Üstün,Matthias Gallé,Tom Sherborne*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 研究发现当前基于LLM的智能体缺乏环境好奇心，即使发现意外但相关的任务解决方案，也无法有效利用这些信息，存在发现与利用之间的显著差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体本应能够将环境观察整合到推理中，但研究发现它们实际上难以反映或应对意外信息，这揭示了当前智能体架构的根本缺陷。

Method: 在三个基准测试(Terminal-Bench、SWE-Bench、AppWorld)中注入完整任务解决方案，故意将解决方案暴露给模型，然后测量智能体发现和利用这些解决方案的比例。

Result: 智能体在Terminal-Bench中发现解决方案的比例为79-81%，但利用比例仅为37-50%；在AppWorld中，超过90%的尝试中看到解决方案文档，但利用比例低于7%。

Conclusion: 当前智能体缺乏环境好奇心，主要受工具可用性、测试时计算和训练数据分布影响。即使优化配置，大多数情况下智能体仍会忽略发现的解决方案。

Abstract: LLM-based agents are assumed to integrate environmental observations into their reasoning: discovering highly relevant but unexpected information should naturally lead to a model exploiting its own discoveries. We show that this assumption is false for current LLM-based agents, which struggle to reflect or react to unexpected information. Across three benchmarks (Terminal-Bench, SWE-Bench, AppWorld), we inject complete task solutions into the agent environments to deliberately expose a task's solution to a model. While agents discover these solutions on Terminal-Bench in 79-81% of runs, they interact, or exploit, them in only 37-50% of cases. This gap is starkest in AppWorld: agents see documentation stating that a command "returns the complete solution to this task" in over 90% of attempts but exploit this in fewer than 7% of trials. We show that agents lack what we call environmental curiosity: the capability to recognize and investigate unexpected but relevant observations in response to environmental stimuli. We identify three main factors influencing environmental curiosity: available tools in the agent scaffold, test-time compute, and training data distribution. Our findings identify configurations that maximize curiosity also achieve the best performance on the unmodified benchmarks. Yet even jointly optimized agents still ignore discovered solutions in the majority of trials: current agents use the environment to fetch expected information, but not to revise their strategy or maximally exploit useful stimuli.

</details>


### [25] [Measuring Distribution Shift in User Prompts and Its Effects on LLM Performance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17650)
*Parker Seegmiller,Sarah Masud Preum*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文提出LENS框架，用于量化自然提示分布偏移对部署LLMs性能的影响，发现用户提示行为的适度偏移会导致性能大幅下降（平均73%损失）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLMs在动态现实环境中部署时，用户提示分布会随时间、用户群体和地理区域发生显著变化，这种自然提示分布偏移对LLM可靠性构成重大挑战，特别是针对特定领域或用户群体的专用模型。目前缺乏对自然提示分布偏移的测量方法及其对部署LLMs影响的研究。

Method: 提出LLM Evaluation under Natural prompt Shift (LENS)框架，这是一种数据驱动的方法，用于量化自然提示分布偏移并评估其对部署LLMs性能的影响。在大规模评估中，使用192个真实世界部署后提示偏移设置，涵盖时间、用户群体和地理三个维度，训练81个模型（使用468万训练提示），并在5.76万提示上进行评估。

Result: 研究发现：1）用户提示行为的适度偏移会导致部署LLMs性能大幅下降（平均73%损失）；2）性能下降在不同潜在用户群体和地理区域交互时尤为普遍；3）性能下降与时间上的自然提示分布偏移相关；4）系统性地描述了LLM指令跟随能力如何随时间推移和用户群体间退化。

Conclusion: 研究结果强调了数据驱动监控的迫切需要，以确保LLM性能在不同且不断演变的用户群体中保持稳定。自然提示分布偏移是LLM部署可靠性的关键挑战，需要系统性监测方法。

Abstract: LLMs are increasingly deployed in dynamic, real-world settings, where the distribution of user prompts can shift substantially over time as new tasks, prompts, and users are introduced to a deployed model. Such natural prompt distribution shift poses a major challenge to LLM reliability, particularly for specialized models designed for narrow domains or user populations. Despite attention to out-of-distribution robustness, there is very limited exploration of measuring natural prompt distribution shift in prior work, and its impact on deployed LLMs remains poorly understood. We introduce the LLM Evaluation under Natural prompt Shift (LENS) framework: a data-centric approach for quantifying natural prompt distribution shift and evaluating its effect on the performance of deployed LLMs. We perform a large-scale evaluation using 192 real-world post-deployment prompt shift settings over time, user group, and geographic axes, training a total of 81 models on 4.68M training prompts, and evaluating on 57.6k prompts. We find that even moderate shifts in user prompt behavior correspond with large performance drops (73% average loss) in deployed LLMs. This performance degradation is particularly prevalent when users from different latent groups and geographic regions interact with models and is correlated with natural prompt distribution shift over time. We systematically characterize how LLM instruction following ability degrades over time and between user groups. Our findings highlight the critical need for data-driven monitoring to ensure LLM performance remains stable across diverse and evolving user populations.

*Jon-Paul Cacioli*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 将临床人格评估中的效度量表框架应用于LLM评估，通过元认知探针数据识别模型回答的有效性，发现部分模型存在构造层面无效的问题


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床人格评估会先检查回答的有效性再解释实质量表，而当前的LLM评估缺乏类似的效度筛查机制，可能导致对模型性能的错误解读

Method: 从PAI和MMPI-3临床评估工具中借鉴效度量表框架，应用于20个前沿模型的524个项目元认知探针数据，操作化六个效度指标：L、K、F、Fp、RBS和TRIN，建立分层分类系统

Result: 识别出4个模型为构造层面无效，2个为升高风险；有效模型能产生项目敏感的置信度（平均r=0.18），而无效模型则不能（平均r=-0.20）；思维链训练产生两种相反的回答扭曲；两个潜在维度解释了94.6%的指标变异

Conclusion: LLM评估需要效度筛查机制，临床心理学中的效度量表框架可有效识别模型回答的有效性问题，为可靠的模型评估提供重要工具

Abstract: Clinical personality assessment screens response validity before interpreting substantive scales. LLM evaluation does not. We apply the validity scaling framework from the PAI and MMPI-3 to metacognitive probe data from 20 frontier models across 524 items. Six validity indices are operationalised: L (maintaining confidence on errors), K (betting on errors), F (withdrawing consensus-endorsed items), Fp (withdrawing correct answers), RBS (inverted monitoring), and TRIN (fixed responding). A tiered classification system identifies four models as construct-level invalid and two as elevated. Valid-profile models produce item-sensitive confidence (mean r = .18, 14 of 16 significant). Invalid-profile models do not (mean r = -.20, d = 2.17, p = .001). Chain-of-thought training produces two opposite response distortions. Two latent dimensions account for 94.6% of index variance. Companion papers extract a portable screening protocol (Cacioli, 2026e) and validate it against selective prediction (Cacioli, 2026f). All data and code: https://github.com/synthiumjp/validity-scaling-llm

### [27] [Screen Before You Interpret: A Portable Validity Protocol for Benchmark-Based LLM Confidence Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17714)
*Jon-Paul Cacioli*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于临床人格评估原则的LLM置信度信号有效性筛查协议，通过三个核心指标、一个结构指标和项目敏感性统计量来评估置信度信号是否携带项目级信息，并在多个基准测试中验证了该协议的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM的置信度信号被用于弃权、路由和安全关键决策，但目前缺乏标准方法来检查置信度信号是否携带项目级信息。需要一种可移植的协议来评估LLM置信度数据的有效性。

Method: 从临床人格评估（PAI、MMPI-3）中转移有效性筛查原则，提出一个包含三个核心指标（L、Fp、RBS）、一个结构指标（TRIN）和项目敏感性统计量的协议，基于单个2x2列联表计算，采用三级分类系统（无效、不确定、有效）。

Result: 在20个前沿LLM和524个项目上验证，4个模型被分类为无效，2个为不确定。有效配置文件模型显示平均r=0.18（15/16显著），无效配置文件模型显示平均r=-0.20（d=2.48）。在MMLU基准和外部数据上的跨基准验证确认了该筛查方法的可移植性。

Conclusion: 提出的有效性筛查协议能够可靠地识别LLM置信度信号是否携带项目级信息，为构建可靠的置信度应用提供了标准化评估框架。

Abstract: LLM confidence signals are used for abstention, routing, and safety-critical decisions. No standard practice exists for checking whether a confidence signal carries item-level information before building on it. We transfer the validity screening principle from clinical personality assessment (PAI, MMPI-3) as a portable protocol for benchmark-based LLM confidence data. The protocol specifies three core indices (L, Fp, RBS), a structural indicator (TRIN), and an item-sensitivity statistic, computed from a single 2x2 contingency table. A three-tier classification system (Invalid, Indeterminate, Valid) draws on four clinical traditions. Validated on 20 frontier LLMs across 524 items, four models are classified Invalid, two Indeterminate. Valid-profile models show mean r = .18 (15/16 significant). Invalid-profile models show mean r = -.20 (d = 2.48). Cross-benchmark validation on 18 models using MMLU with verbalized confidence and on external data from Yang et al. (2024) confirms the screen transfers across benchmarks and probe formats. All data and code: https://github.com/synthiumjp/validity-scaling-llm

### [28] [Concurrent Criterion Validation of a Validity Screen for LLM Confidence Signals via Selective Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17716)
*Jon-Paul Cacioli*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用有效性筛选将20个前沿LLM的置信度信号分类为有效、不确定和无效三类，在524个项目上评估六个认知轨迹的选择性预测性能，采用Type 2 AUROC指标，并进行分半交叉验证。

Result: 有效模型平均AUROC为0.624，无效模型为0.357，效应量d=2.81，p=0.002；三个层级呈现单调排序：无效(0.357)<不确定(0.554)<有效(0.624)；分类解释了AUROC方差的47%。

Conclusion: 有效性筛选分类能有效预测选择性预测性能，对于选择性预测任务来说，置信度信号的有效性筛选至关重要。

Valid models show mean Type 2 AUROC = .624 (SD = .048). Invalid models show mean AUROC = .357 (SD = .231). Cohen's d = 2.81, p = .002. The tiers order monotonically: Invalid (.357) < Indeterminate (.554) < Valid (.624). Split-half cross-validation yields median d = 1.77, P(d > 0) = 1.0 across 1,000 splits. The three-tier classification accounts for 47% of the variance in AUROC. DeepSeek-R1 drops from 85.3% accuracy at full coverage to 11.3% at 10% coverage. The screen predicts the criterion. For selective prediction, the screen matters.

Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) acts as a critical "reasoning unlocker", yielding a 77% improvement in Explanation Quality and bridging the gap between raw calculation and pedagogical coherence. Furthermore, our analysis of prompting strategies uncovers a significant trade-off: structured frameworks like ReAct impose a "cognitive tax" on the 1.7B parameter capacity, degrading performance relative to pure Chain-of-Thought (CoT) combined with Self-Consistency. These findings establish a deployment hierarchy for SLMs, demonstrating that SFT combined with simplified test-time scaling is superior to complex agentic workflows for edge-based reasoning.

We further systematically investigate how collaboration strategies are shaped by SLM and LLM capabilities as well as efficiency and privacy constraints. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入QuickScope方法，基于COUP贝叶斯优化算法进行实质性修改以适应实际LLM流程，并包装成支持灵活选择数据集和效用函数的工具，用户可以针对特定类型的问题（如低准确率问题、相对于测量复杂度异常困难的问题）。

Result: 在多个基准测试实验中，QuickScope比标准基线方法更高效地发现真正困难的问题，同时减少噪声结果导致的误报。

Abstract: LLM benchmarks are increasingly dynamic: instead of containing a fixed set of questions, they define templates and parameters that can generate an effectively unlimited number of question variants. This flexibility is valuable, but it makes evaluation expensive -- especially when the goal is not just determining an average score, but reliably identifying a model's weak spots. This paper introduces a new methodology for identifying hard questions in dynamic benchmarks. It leverages COUP, a recent Bayesian optimization algorithm (Graham, Velez & Leyton-Brown, 2026), after introducing several substantive modifications to make the algorithm suitable for practical LLM pipelines. We also wrap it in a tool that supports flexible choices of datasets and utility functions, enabling users to target the kinds of questions they care about (e.g., low-accuracy questions; questions that are unusually hard relative to their measured complexity). In experiments across a range of benchmarks, we show that our method, dubbed $\texttt{QuickScope}$, discovers truly difficult questions more sample efficiently than standard baselines, while also reducing false positives from noisy outcomes.

### [33] [GraSP: Graph-Structured Skill Compositions for LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17870)
*Tianle Xia,Lingxiang Hu,Yiding Sun,Ming Xu,Lan Xu,Siying Wang,Wei Xu,Jie Jiang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: GraSP提出首个可执行技能图架构，通过编译层将平面技能集转换为类型化有向无环图，实现结构化编排而非更多技能，显著提升LLM智能体性能


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM智能体技能生态系统已成熟，但研究表明提供更多技能并不能单调提升性能，甚至可能损害表现。瓶颈已从技能可用性转向技能编排：智能体需要的不是更多技能，而是选择、组合和执行技能的结构化机制

Method: 提出GraSP架构，引入技能检索与执行之间的编译层，将平面技能集转换为具有前提条件-效果边的类型化有向无环图，执行时进行节点级验证，并通过五种类型化操作符进行局部有界修复，将重规划复杂度从O(N)降至O(d^h)

Result: 在ALFWorld、ScienceWorld、WebShop和InterCode等八个LLM骨干网络上，GraSP在所有配置中均优于ReAct、Reflexion、ExpeL和平面技能基线，奖励提升高达+19分，环境步骤减少高达41%。优势随任务复杂度增加而增强，对技能过度检索和质量退化具有鲁棒性

Conclusion: 结构化编排而非更大的技能库是实现可靠智能体执行的关键。GraSP通过可执行技能图架构有效解决了技能编排瓶颈，为LLM智能体提供了更高效的任务执行框架

Abstract: Skill ecosystems for LLM agents have matured rapidly, yet recent benchmarks show that providing agents with more skills does not monotonically improve performance -- focused sets of 2-3 skills outperform comprehensive documentation, and excessive skills actually hurt. The bottleneck has shifted from skill availability to skill orchestration: agents need not more skills, but a structural mechanism to select, compose, and execute them with explicit causal dependencies. We propose GraSP, the first executable skill graph architecture that introduces a compilation layer between skill retrieval and execution. GraSP transforms flat skill sets into typed directed acyclic graphs (DAGs) with precondition-effect edges, executes them with node-level verification, and performs locality-bounded repair through five typed operators -- reducing replanning from O(N) to O(d^h). Across ALFWorld, ScienceWorld, WebShop, and InterCode with eight LLM backbones, GraSP outperforms ReAct, Reflexion, ExpeL, and flat skill baselines in every configuration, improving reward by up to +19 points over the strongest baseline while cutting environment steps by up to 41%. GraSP's advantage grows with task complexity and is robust to both skill over-retrieval and quality degradation, confirming that structured orchestration -- not larger skill libraries -- is the key to reliable agent execution.

</details>

To study this problem, we introduce MPT, a benchmark comprising 265 multi-session dialogues that cover three challenges: Preference Recall, Preference Induction, and Preference Transfer. We also propose PRefine, a test-time memory-augmented method that represents user preferences as evolving hypotheses. Through a generate--verify--refine loop, it extracts reusable constraints from history and improves tool-calling accuracy while using only 1.24% of the tokens required by full-history prompting. These results indicate that robust personalization in agentic systems depends on memory that captures the reasons behind user choices, not just the choices themselves.

### [36] [Copy-as-Decode: Grammar-Constrained Parallel Prefill for LLM Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18170)
*Ziyang Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出Copy-as-Decode机制，将编辑生成重构为结构化解码，通过并行预填充而非自回归生成来加速文本/代码编辑，显著提升速度并保持高覆盖率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLMs在编辑文本和代码时，即使大部分标记与输入相同，仍采用自回归方式重新生成完整输出，导致效率低下。需要一种机制来避免不必要的重新生成，提高编辑效率。

Method: 提出Copy-as-Decode解码层机制，使用两种基本原语的语法：<copy lines="i-j"/>引用输入行范围，<gen>...</gen>生成新内容。通过令牌级FSM保证语法有效性，服务层原语通过单次并行预填充前向传播更新KV缓存，而非N次自回归步骤。

Result: 1) 内核加速：在Qwen2.5模型上，通过并行预填充复制N个标记比自回归快6.8×-303×；2) 复制覆盖率：在ProbeEdit和HumanEvalPack-Fix数据集上，74%-98%的金标记可通过行级原语达到；3) 管道无损性：所有482个案例通过确定性解析器往返，下游失败仅源于范围选择而非机制本身。

Conclusion: Copy-as-Decode机制能显著加速LLMs的编辑任务，通过结构化解码和并行预填充实现高效编辑，具有高覆盖率和学习能力信号，为实际部署提供了理论基础。

Abstract: LLMs edit text and code by autoregressively regenerating the full output, even when most tokens appear verbatim in the input. We study Copy-as-Decode, a decoding-layer mechanism that recasts edit generation as structured decoding over a two-primitive grammar: <copy lines="i-j"/> references an input line range, <gen>...</gen> emits new content. A token-level FSM guarantees syntactic validity, and a serving-layer primitive updates the KV cache for each copy span via a single parallel-prefill forward rather than $N$ autoregressive steps -- sharing the parallel-forward kernel of speculative decoding but with input tokens as the draft and program-enforced acceptance replacing probabilistic verification. We report an upper-bound analysis that requires no end-to-end training. (i) Kernel speedup: on Qwen2.5-{1.5B, 7B}, copying $N$ tokens via parallel prefill is $6.8\times$--$303\times$ faster than autoregressive ($N \in [8, 512]$, A100 80GB bf16). (ii) Copy ceiling: on ProbeEdit and HumanEvalPack-Fix (Py/JS), $74$--$98\%$ of gold tokens are reachable under the line-level primitive; composed with the empirical kernel over each corpus's span histogram this yields a closed-form wall-clock bound of $29.0\times / 3.4\times / 4.2\times$ ($13.0\times$ pooled). A token-level extension reaches $91$--$99\%$ coverage with $4.5\times$--$6.5\times$ floors. (iii) Pipeline losslessness: oracle programs round-trip through the deterministic resolver on all $482$ cases, localizing any downstream failure to span selection rather than the mechanism. A perturbation study shows pooled EM drops from $100\%$ to $15.48\%$ under off-by-one noise. A fine-tuning pilot on Qwen2.5-Coder-1.5B lifts HEvalFix-Py EM from $0/33$ (untrained) to $12$--$17\%$, a learnability signal, not a production selector. Batched-serving integration and multi-file coverage are scoped as follow-up.

</details>


### [37] [STaD: Scaffolded Task Design for Identifying Compositional Skill Gaps in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18177)
*Sungeun An,Swanand Ravindra Kadhe,Shailja Thakur,Chad DeLuca,Hima Patel*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出STaD框架，通过脚手架任务设计生成基准任务的受控变体，系统性地探测LLM在组合推理技能上的缺陷，而非仅关注总体基准分数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试的聚合分数只能提供有限信息，无法揭示LLM在组合推理技能上的具体缺陷以及如何改进这些缺陷。

Method: 提出脚手架任务设计（STaD）框架，基于脚手架概念生成基准任务的受控变体，通过结构化、渐进的支持步骤，系统性地探测模型行为。

Result: 在六个不同规模的模型上进行实验，在三个推理基准测试中发现了多个失败点，并突出了每个模型独特且不同的技能缺陷。

Conclusion: STaD框架能够系统且可扩展地探测LLM行为，识别其缺乏的具体推理技能组合，为理解模型能力提供了更深入的洞察。

Abstract: Benchmarks are often used as a standard to understand LLM capabilities in different domains. However, aggregate benchmark scores provide limited insight into compositional skill gaps of LLMs and how to improve them. To make these weaknesses visible, we propose Scaffolded Task Design (STaD) framework. STaD generates controlled variations of benchmark tasks based on the concept of scaffolding, which introduces structured, incremental support in a step-by-step manner. Rather than inspecting failures individually, this approach enables systematic and scalable probing of model behavior by identifying the specific reasoning skill compositions they lack. Treating the LLM as a black box, our experiments on six models of varying sizes reveal multiple failure points in three reasoning benchmarks and highlight each model's unique and distinct skill gaps.

</details>


### [38] [Negative Advantage Is a Double-Edged Sword: Calibrating Advantage in GRPO for Deep Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18235)
*Jiayi Wu,Ruobing Xie,Zeqian Huang,Lei Jiang,Can Xu,Kangyang Luo,Ming Gao,Xiang Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了CalibAdv方法，通过校准优势函数来解决深度搜索代理训练中的中间步骤误惩罚和训练不稳定问题


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的GRPO算法在深度搜索任务中存在两个主要问题：1）中间步骤正确性与最终奖励信号不匹配，导致正确中间步骤被错误惩罚；2）训练不稳定，容易导致自然语言能力退化甚至训练崩溃

Method: 提出CalibAdv优势校准方法：1）利用中间步骤的正确性在细粒度层面缩减过度的负优势；2）在答案组件中重新平衡正负优势

Result: 在三个模型和七个基准测试上的广泛实验表明，CalibAdv提高了模型性能和训练稳定性

Conclusion: CalibAdv通过精细化的优势校准有效解决了深度搜索代理训练中的关键问题，提升了训练效果和稳定性

Abstract: Deep search agents can autonomously initiate multi-turn interactions with search engines, thereby exhibiting strong question-answering capabilities. Such performance critically relies on Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) as its core training algorithm. However, GRPO still faces several challenges in deep search settings. First, there exists a substantial mismatch between the correctness of intermediate steps and the reward signal, causing numerous correct intermediate steps to be incorrectly penalized when the final answer is wrong. Second, training is highly unstable, often resulting in degradation of natural language ability or even catastrophic training collapse. Our analysis attributes these issues to coarse-grained advantage assignment and an imbalance between positive and negative advantages. To address these problems, we propose CalibAdv, an advantage calibration method specifically designed for deep search tasks. Specifically, CalibAdv leverages the correctness of intermediate steps to downscale excessive negative advantages at a fine-grained level. It then rebalances positive and negative advantages in the answer component. Extensive experiments across three models and seven benchmarks demonstrate that CalibAdv improves both model performance and training stability. Our code is available at https://github.com/wujwyi/CalibAdv.

### [39] [Exploring Concreteness Through a Figurative Lens](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18296)
*Saptarshi Ghosh,Tianyu Jiang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LLMs在早期层区分字面与比喻用法，中后期层将具体性压缩为一维方向，该方向可用于比喻语言分类和无训练生成控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 静态具体性评分在NLP中广泛使用，但词语的具体性会随上下文变化（尤其在比喻语言中）。虽然上下文能显示这种变化，但LLM内部如何理解具体性仍不清楚。

Method: 对四个模型家族的LLM隐藏表示进行分层和几何分析，研究模型如何区分同一名词的字面与比喻用法，以及具体性在表示空间中的组织方式。

Result: LLMs在早期层分离字面和比喻用法，中后期层将具体性压缩为一致的一维方向。该几何结构可用于高效的比喻语言分类和无训练生成控制。

Conclusion: LLMs内部形成了稳定的具体性几何结构，该结构具有实际应用价值，支持高效的比喻语言处理任务。

Abstract: Static concreteness ratings are widely used in NLP, yet a word's concreteness can shift with context, especially in figurative language such as metaphor, where common concrete nouns can take abstract interpretations. While such shifts are evident from context, it remains unclear how LLMs understand concreteness internally. We conduct a layer-wise and geometric analysis of LLM hidden representations across four model families, examining how models distinguish literal vs figurative uses of the same noun and how concreteness is organized in representation space. We find that LLMs separate literal and figurative usage in early layers, and that mid-to-late layers compress concreteness into a one-dimensional direction that is consistent across models. Finally, we show that this geometric structure is practically useful: a single concreteness direction supports efficient figurative-language classification and enables training-free steering of generation toward more literal or more figurative rewrites.

### [40] [HiGMem: A Hierarchical and LLM-Guided Memory System for Long-Term Conversational Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18349)
*Shuqi Cao,Jingyi He,Fei Tan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: HiGMem是一个分层且LLM引导的记忆系统，通过事件摘要作为语义锚点，让LLM预测哪些相关对话轮次值得阅读，从而提供简洁可靠的证据集，避免向量检索的膨胀问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆系统（包括分层系统）主要依赖向量相似性进行检索，这会导致证据集膨胀：添加许多表面相似的对话轮次几乎不会增加召回率，但会降低检索精度、增加答案阶段的上下文成本，并使检索到的记忆更难检查和管理。

Method: 提出HiGMem（分层和LLM引导的记忆系统），这是一个两级事件-轮次记忆系统，允许LLM使用事件摘要作为语义锚点来预测哪些相关轮次值得阅读。模型先检查高级事件摘要，然后聚焦于较小的潜在有用轮次集合。

Result: 在LoCoMo10基准测试中，HiGMem在五个问题类别中的四个上取得了最佳F1分数，并将对抗性F1从A-Mem的0.54提高到0.78，同时检索的轮次数量减少了一个数量级。

Conclusion: HiGMem通过LLM引导的推理提供简洁可靠的证据集，避免了向量检索的过度开销，显著提高了长期对话LLM代理的记忆检索性能。

Abstract: Long-term conversational large language model (LLM) agents require memory systems that can recover relevant evidence from historical interactions without overwhelming the answer stage with irrelevant context. However, existing memory systems, including hierarchical ones, still often rely solely on vector similarity for retrieval. It tends to produce bloated evidence sets: adding many superficially similar dialogue turns yields little additional recall, but lowers retrieval precision, increases answer-stage context cost, and makes retrieved memories harder to inspect and manage. To address this, we propose HiGMem (Hierarchical and LLM-Guided Memory System), a two-level event-turn memory system that allows LLMs to use event summaries as semantic anchors to predict which related turns are worth reading. This allows the model to inspect high-level event summaries first and then focus on a smaller set of potentially useful turns, providing a concise and reliable evidence set through reasoning, while avoiding the retrieval overhead that would be excessively high compared to vector retrieval. On the LoCoMo10 benchmark, HiGMem achieves the best F1 on four of five question categories and improves adversarial F1 from 0.54 to 0.78 over A-Mem, while retrieving an order of magnitude fewer turns. Code is publicly available at https://github.com/ZeroLoss-Lab/HiGMem.

</details>


### [41] [ComPASS: Towards Personalized Agentic Social Support via Tool-Augmented Companionship](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18356)

Conclusion: 工具增强的LLM代理能够提供更实质性的社会支持，ComPASS框架在个性化社会支持任务上表现出色，为开发更具同理心的交互系统提供了新方向。

Abstract: Developing compassionate interactive systems requires agents to not only understand user emotions but also provide diverse, substantive support. While recent works explore empathetic dialogue generation, they remain limited in response form and content, struggling to satisfy diverse needs across users and contexts. To address this, we explore empowering agents with external tools to execute diverse actions. Grounded in the psychological concept of "social support", this paradigm delivers substantive, human-like companionship. Specifically, we first design a dozen user-centric tools simulating various multimedia applications, which can cover different types of social support behaviors in human-agent interaction scenarios. We then construct ComPASS-Bench, the first personalized social support benchmark for LLM-based agents, via multi-step automated synthesis and manual refinement. Based on ComPASS-Bench, we further synthesize tool use records to fine-tune the Qwen3-8B model, yielding a task-specific ComPASS-Qwen. Comprehensive evaluations across two settings reveal that while the evaluated LLMs can generate valid tool-calling requests with high success rates, significant gaps remain in final response quality. Moreover, tool-augmented responses achieve better overall performance than directly producing conversational empathy. Notably, our trained ComPASS-Qwen demonstrates substantial improvements over its base model, achieving comparable performance to several large-scale models. Our code and data are available at https://github.com/hzp3517/ComPASS.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对话系统主要关注对话过程中的激活，忽视了对话启动阶段的瓶颈。用户在对话开始时可能有模糊需求但没有明确查询意图，形成"首消息障碍"，导致对话无法开始。

Method: 提出IceBreaker框架，将人类破冰过程建模为两步握手：(1)通过会话摘要进行共鸣感知的兴趣提取，捕捉触发兴趣；(2)通过交互导向的开场白生成，结合个性化偏好对齐和自增强循环优化用户参与度。

Result: 在全球最大的对话代理产品上进行在线A/B测试，结果显示IceBreaker将用户活跃天数提升+0.184%，点击率提升+9.425%，并已部署到生产环境。

Abstract: Conversational agents, such as ChatGPT and Doubao, have become essential daily assistants for billions of users. To further enhance engagement, these systems are evolving from passive responders to proactive companions. However, existing efforts focus on activation within ongoing dialogues, while overlooking a key real-world bottleneck. In the conversation initiation stage, users may have a vague need but no explicit query intent, creating a first-message barrier where the conversation holds before it begins. To overcome this, we introduce Conversation Starter Generation: generating personalized starters to guide users into conversation. However, unlike in-conversation stages where immediate context guides the response, initiation must operate in a cold-start moment without explicit user intent. To pioneer in this direction, we present IceBreaker that frames human ice-breaking as a two-step handshake: (i) evoke resonance via Resonance-Aware Interest Distillation from session summaries to capture trigger interests, and (ii) stimulate interaction via Interaction-Oriented Starter Generation, optimized with personalized preference alignment and a self-reinforced loop to maximize engagement. Online A/B tests on one of the world's largest conversational agent products show that IceBreaker improves user active days by +0.184% and click-through rate by +9.425%, and has been deployed in production.

### [43] [Understanding the Prompt Sensitivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18389)
*Yang Liu,Chenhui Chu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文通过将LLMs视为多元函数并进行一阶泰勒展开，分析了意义保留提示、梯度与模型下一个token对数概率之间的关系，揭示了LLMs内部不聚类相似输入而是分散它们，导致意义相同提示间的对数概率差异难以有效降低，解释了当前LLMs对提示高度敏感的原因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 提示敏感性（prompt sensitivity）指LLM输出对输入提示确切措辞的依赖程度，这引发了用户对LLM稳定性和可靠性的担忧。本文旨在理解为什么当前LLMs对意义相同的提示会表现出高度敏感性。

Method: 将LLMs视为多元函数，进行一阶泰勒展开，分析意义保留提示、梯度与模型下一个token对数概率之间的关系。使用柯西-施瓦茨不等式推导对数概率差异的上界。分析logit方差，比较提示模板与问题本身对logits的影响。

Result: 发现LLMs内部不聚类相似输入而是分散它们，导致意义相同提示间的对数概率差异上界过高且难以有效降低。识别了哪些类型的意义保留提示变体更容易引入提示敏感性风险。上界与现有指标PromptSensiScore强相关。提示模板通常比问题本身对logits影响更大。

Conclusion: 研究结果为理解当前LLMs对意义相同提示高度敏感的现象提供了通用解释和关键证据，有助于深入理解LLMs的提示敏感性机制。

Abstract: Prompt sensitivity, which refers to how strongly the output of a large language model (LLM) depends on the exact wording of its input prompt, raises concerns among users about the LLM's stability and reliability. In this work, we consider LLMs as multivariate functions and perform a first-order Taylor expansion, thereby analyzing the relationship between meaning-preserving prompts, their gradients, and the log probabilities of the model's next token. We derive an upper bound on the difference between log probabilities using the Cauchy-Schwarz inequality. We show that LLMs do not internally cluster similar inputs like smaller neural networks do, but instead disperse them. This dispersing behavior leads to an excessively high upper bound on the difference of log probabilities between two meaning-preserving prompts, making it difficult to effectively reduce to 0. In our analysis, we also show which types of meaning-preserving prompt variants are more likely to introduce prompt sensitivity risks in LLMs. In addition, we demonstrate that the upper bound is strongly correlated with an existing prompt sensitivity metric, PromptSensiScore. Moreover, by analyzing the logit variance, we find that prompt templates typically exert a greater influence on logits than the questions themselves. Overall, our results provide a general interpretation for why current LLMs can be highly sensitive to prompts with the same meaning, offering crucial evidence for understanding the prompt sensitivity of LLMs. Code for experiments is available at https://github.com/ku-nlp/Understanding_the_Prompt_Sensitivity.

</details>


### [44] [StepPO: Step-Aligned Policy Optimization for Agentic Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18401)
*Daoyu Wang,Qingchuan Li,Mingyue Cheng,Jie Ouyang,Shuo Yu,Qi Liu,Enhong Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: StepPO提出将Agentic RL从传统的token级MDP推进到step级MDP，认为step而非token才是LLM智能体的合适动作表示，并提出了step级信用分配作为优化对应


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着通用智能体系统追求更宏大目标，对基础LLM的智能体能力要求越来越高。传统的token级建模和优化范式在捕捉真实LLM智能体行为方面越来越不足，特别是在多轮交互、延迟稀疏奖励、长变长上下文等挑战下

Method: 提出step级Agentic RL范式：1）将传统token级MDP推进到step级MDP；2）将step而非token视为LLM智能体的合适动作表示；3）提出step级信用分配作为优化对应；4）讨论了实现step级Agentic RL的关键系统设计

Result: 初步实验为这一视角的有效性提供了初步证据，表明step对齐的step级范式有助于理解智能体行为并推进LLM向更强的通用智能体能力发展

Conclusion: StepPO提出的step对齐、step级范式为Agentic RL社区提供了理解智能体行为的有用视角，有助于推进LLM向更强的通用智能体能力发展

Abstract: General agents have given rise to phenomenal applications such as OpenClaw and Claude Code. As these agent systems (a.k.a. Harnesses) strive for bolder goals, they demand increasingly stronger agentic capabilities from foundation Large Language Models (LLMs). Agentic Reinforcement Learning (RL) is emerging as a central post-training paradigm for empowering LLMs with these capabilities and is playing an increasingly pivotal role in agent training. Unlike single-turn token-level alignment or reasoning enhancement, as in RLHF and RLVR, Agentic RL targets multi-turn interactive settings, where the goal is to optimize core agentic capabilities such as decision making and tool use while addressing new challenges including delayed and sparse rewards, as well as long and variable context. As a result, the token-centric modeling and optimization paradigm inherited from traditional LLM RL is becoming increasingly inadequate for capturing real LLM agent behavior. In this paper, we present StepPO as a position on step-level Agentic RL. We argue that the conventional token-level Markov Decision Process (MDP) should be advanced to a step-level MDP formulation, and that the step, rather than the token, should be regarded as the proper action representation for LLM agents. We then propose step-level credit assignment as the natural optimization counterpart of this formulation, thereby aligning policy optimization and reward propagation with the granularity of agent decisions. Finally, we discuss the key systems designs required to realize step-level Agentic RL in practice and preliminary experiments provide initial evidence for the effectiveness of this perspective. We hope that the step-aligned, step-level paradigm embodied in StepPO offers the Agentic RL community a useful lens for understanding agent behavior and helps advance LLMs toward stronger general-agent capabilities.

</details>

### [45] [Software Self-Extension with SelfEvolve: an Agentic Architecture for Runtime Code Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16314)
*Md Asif Iqbal Fahim,Oluwadamilola Adebayo,Alessio Ferrari*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: SelfEvolve是一种基于LLM的自主代码生成架构，能够在运行时自动扩展系统功能，实现超越传统自适应系统的自我进化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出SelfEvolve架构，采用编排的代理管道实现运行时自我扩展。系统能够基于用户请求自主生成新功能代码并集成到运行系统中，无需系统重启或开发者干预。

Result: 在11个自我扩展任务上的评估显示，平均Pass@1达到92.7%（51/55），显著优于AutoGen、MetaGPT和AgentCoder等基线方法，比最佳基线AutoGen提升61.8%，具有统计显著性。

Conclusion: 证明了通过自主代码生成实现运行时能力扩展的可行性，为系统自主进化以满足用户需求的新范式提供了初步证据，为个性化、自我改进系统铺平了道路。

Abstract: Traditional self-adaptive systems automatically reconfigure existing components in response to changing requirements, but provide limited support for the generation of novel functionalities. The software generation capabilities of large language models (LLMs) open the possibility to create entirely new modules at runtime, enabling a form of self-evolution beyond traditional self-adaptation. We present SelfEvolve, an orchestrated agentic pipeline architecture enabling runtime self-extension--the autonomous addition of new capabilities during execution--as a preliminary form of self-evolution. Self-extension focuses on the autonomous generation and integration of new functions, based on user requests, without requiring a system restart or developer intervention. Evaluation of our architecture across 11 self-extension tasks demonstrates an average Pass@1 of 92.7% (51/55), outperforming developer-focused code generation baselines like AutoGen, MetaGPT, and AgentCoder. SelfEvolve achieves 61.8% improvement over the best baseline, i.e. Autogen, with statistical significance. This work demonstrates the feasibility of runtime capability extension through autonomous code generation. This provides preliminary evidence for a paradigm in which systems autonomously evolve to satisfy user needs, paving the way towards individualised, self-improving systems.

### [46] [How Robustly do LLMs Understand Execution Semantics?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16320)
*Claudio Spiess,Prem Devanbu,Earl T. Barr*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 论文研究LLM在代码理解中的鲁棒性，发现前沿模型GPT-5.2在代码扰动下准确率显著下降（从99%降至75-79%），而开源推理模型表现更稳定但准确率较低。研究还发现模型在预测异常行为方面表现不佳，并探索了改进方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究LLM是否使用内部世界模型还是依赖模式匹配，通过代码理解的鲁棒性来探究这一问题。使用程序输出预测任务来评估模型在代码变换和输入扰动下的表现。

Method: 采用标准程序输出预测任务，在CRUXEval基准测试上进行实验。对代码进行变换和输入扰动，比较不同模型在原始和扰动输入下的表现。特别关注模型预测异常行为的能力，并探索改进异常预测的方法。

Result: GPT-5.2在原始CRUXEval上达到99%准确率，但在扰动输入下准确率下降20-24%。开源推理模型（DeepSeek-R1系列）表现更稳定但准确率较低（38-67%）。模型在预测异常行为方面表现不佳，且性能取决于异常类型。

Conclusion: 所有模型在代码理解方面都存在局限性，使用扰动评估代码模型具有重要价值。研究揭示了前沿模型在鲁棒性方面的脆弱性，为改进代码理解模型提供了方向。

Abstract: LLMs demonstrate remarkable reasoning capabilities, yet whether they utilize internal world models or rely on sophisticated pattern matching remains open. We study LLMs through the lens of robustness of their code understanding using a standard program-output prediction task. Our results reveal a stark divergence in model behavior: while open-source reasoning models (DeepSeek-R1 family) maintain stable, albeit somewhat lower accuracies (38% to 67%) under code transformations & input perturbations, the frontier model GPT-5.2 exhibits significant brittleness. Despite achieving a near-perfect score of 99% on the original, unperturbed CRUXEval benchmark, perturbed inputs trigger accuracy declines between 20% and 24%. In addition, we find that many models perform much worse at predicting behavior on perturbed inputs that raise exceptions, and that prediction performance depends on the kind of exception. We study remedies to address this deficiency in exception prediction, and evaluate the effect of these remedies on the ability to predict non-exception behaviors. Our findings both point to limitations in the way all models understand code, and establish the value of using perturbation to evaluate code models.

</details>
